event = {
	id = 3182051
	random = no
	country = USA

	# triggered by ENG 3131053 (triggers 1 day after Pearl Harbor event if USA doesn't enter allies manually)

	name = EVT_3182051_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182051_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "usa_allies"

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182051A
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182051B
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { }
	}
}

#########################################################################
# Early war (declaration of war on USA before 1941)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182028
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
				NOT = { local_flag = USA_warmongering }
				under_attack = USA
				}

	name = EVT_3182028_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182028_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "jap_us_protest"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1940 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182028A
		command = { type = build_cost which = naval when = on_upgrade value = 10 where = relative }
		command = { type = build_time which = naval when = on_upgrade value = -10 where = relative }
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = 4688 }
		
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182130 } # USA allowed to enter war because of sea lion
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182001 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. ENG
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182194 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. SOV
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182102 } # warmongering USA, penalty event
	}
}

#########################################################################
# Warmongering USA - penalty event for entering the war prematurely
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182102
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		government = democratic
		atwar = yes
		NOT = { under_attack = USA }
		NOT = {
				OR =	{
						# US invasion
						lost_national = { value = 1 }						
						# JAP attacking ENG only
						AND =	{
								NOT = { ai = ENG }
								NOT = { ai = JAP }
								NOT = { ai = GER }
								NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = USA } }
								}
								war = { country = JAP country = ENG }
								war = { country = ENG country = GER }
								}
						# sea lion
						AND =	{
								war = { country = ENG country = GER }
								NOT = 	{
											ai = ENG
											ai = GER
											war = { country = GER country = USA }
										}
								OR =	{
											NOT = { control = { province = 4 data = ENG }  } # British main island
											NOT = { control = { province = 5 data = ENG }  }
											NOT = { control = { province = 6 data = ENG }  }
											NOT = { control = { province = 7 data = ENG }  }
											NOT = { control = { province = 8 data = ENG }  }
											NOT = { control = { province = 10 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 11 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 12 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 13 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 14 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 15 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 16 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 17 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 18 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 19 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 20 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 21 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 22 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 23 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 24 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 25 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 26 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 27 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 28 data = ENG } }
											NOT = { control = { province = 29 data = ENG } }
										}
								}
						# JAP and SOV at war
						AND = {
								OR = {
										war = { country = SOV country = JAP }
										war = { country = SOV country = U00 }
										}
								war = { country = SOV country = GER }
						
								NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = USA } }
								NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = USA } }
								NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = USA } }		
								NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
								
								NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = JAP } }
								NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = ENG } }
								NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = SOV } }
								NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = GER } }
								
								NOT = { ispuppet = USA }
							}
					}
				}

	name = EVT_3182102_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182102_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "usa_declares_war"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1941 } #1999; after 1942, USA may enter the war without extra penalty

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182102A
		command = { type = dissent value = 20 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = USA_warmongering }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182130 } # USA allowed to enter war because of sea lion
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182194 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. SOV
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182001 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. ENG
		
	}
}

#############################################################################
# USA may enter war ahistorically early in MP when GB or SOV get into big trouble
# split up for different offsets
#############################################################################

event = {
	id = 3182001 # Japan attacking ENG only
	random = no
	country = USA
	
	trigger = {
				NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = ENG } }
				NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = USA } }
				war = { country = JAP country = ENG }
				war = { country = ENG country = GER }
				NOT = { alliance = { country = JAP country = USA } }
				NOT = { ispuppet = USA }
				}
	
	name = EVT_3182001_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182001_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "usa_early_war"
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 7 #enough time for manual diplomatic actions
	deathdate = { day = 6 month = december year = 1963 }
	
	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182001A
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 6 }
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = 400 }
		command = { trigger = { AI = no AI = JAP} type = dissent value = 3 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182130 } # USA allowed to enter war because of sea lion
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182194 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. SOV
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182102 } # warmongering USA, penalty event
#		command = { trigger = { AI = yes } type = alliance which = ENG }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182160B #We need to stay neutral, no matter what the cost!
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = dissent value = 6 }
	}
}

#####################################################################################
# 1942+: USA enter the war because of random sinking of US shipping (USS America)
# (event to finally get USA into the war if Axis decides to not attack
#####################################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182160
	random = no
	country = USA
	
	trigger = {
				war = { country = GER country = ENG }
				NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = USA } }
				NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = USA } }
				NOT = { ispuppet = USA }
				random = 10
				}

	name = EVT_3182160_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182160_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "usa_event_SS_America"

	date = { day = 10 month = february year = 1942 }
	offset = 14
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = january year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182160A #Enough is enough! Britain needs our help!
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 6 }
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = 400 }
		command = { trigger = { AI = no } type = sleepevent which = 3182130 }
		command = { trigger = { AI = no } type = sleepevent which = 3182102 }
		command = { trigger = { AI = no } type = dissent value = 3 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 3182161 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182160B #We need to stay neutral, no matter what the cost!
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = dissent value = 6 }
	}
}

#########################################################################
# New war in Europe, US reaction
# event for unlikely war ENG vs. SOV
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182086
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
		exists = ENG
		war = { country = SOV country = ENG  }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				exists = GER
				ispuppet = SOV
				alliance = { country = USA country = ENG  }
				alliance = { country = USA country = SOV  }
				war = { country = SOV country = USA }
			}
		}
	}

	name = EVT_3182086_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182086_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "usa_war_in_europa"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182086A
		ai_chance = 95
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182130 } # USA allowed to enter war because of sea lion
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182001 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. ENG
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182194 } # USA allowed to enter war because of war JAP vs. SOV
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 3182102 } # warmongering USA, penalty event
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182086B
		ai_chance = 5
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = -1 }
	}
}

#########################################################################
# German Aggression on British Isles, US ultimatum
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182079
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
		random = 30
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				war = { country = USA country = ENG }
				war = { country = USA country = GER }
			}
		}
		OR = {
				NOT = { region = { region = "England" country = ENG }}
				NOT = { region = { region = "Scotland" country = ENG }}
		}
		OR = {
			exists = VIC
			control = { province = 55 data = GER } # Paris
		}
		OR = {
			control = { province = 116 data = GER } # Bruxelles
			control = { province = 207 data = GER } # Prague
			control = { province = 109 data = GER } # Lux
			control = { province = 122 data = GER } # Amsterdam
			control = { province = 294 data = GER } # Copenhagen
			control = { province = 483 data = GER } # Oslo
		}
	}

	name = EVT_3182079_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182079_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "jap_us_protest"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182079A
		command = { type = trigger which = 3136135 } # GER
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182079B
		command = { type = money value = -5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	}
}

#########################################################################
# U.S. "Two-Ocean Navy" Act
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 3182032
	random = no
	country = USA
	
	decision = { atwar = GER }
	
	decision_trigger = {
							#atwar = no
							#headofstate = 6001
							OR = {
									AND = {
											war = { country = GER country = BEL }
											lost_national = { country = BEL value = 1 }
											}
									AND = {
											war = { country = GER country = HOL }
											lost_national = { country = HOL value = 1 }
											}
									AND = {
											war = { country = GER country = LUX }
											lost_national = { country = LUX value = 1 }
											}
									NOT = { exists = CHI }
									puppet = { country = CHI country = JAP }
									war = { country = JAP country = ENG }
									NOT = { control = { province = 55 data = FRA } }

event = {
	id = 3182087
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
		war = { country = USA country = GER }
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }
		war = { country = SOV country = GER }
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
			war = { country = USA country = ENG }
			war = { country = ENG country = SOV }
			war = { country = ENG country = USA }
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { control = { province = 55 data = -2 } } # Paris
			NOT = { control = { province = 232 data = -2 } } # Warsaw
		}
	}

	name = EVT_3182087_NAME
	desc = EVT_3182087_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "yalta"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3182087A
		command = { type = trigger which = 3182088 }
	}
}
